- C = 0.523287159969136
- E = -3.39285482994202 * 0.0780638344630251 ≈ -0.264876...
- D = -0.710540944238196

Note that `sin(t) = cos(t - π/2)`, so `C*sin(t) = C*cos(t - π/2)`.

Now let me check **Candidate 34**: `c0*x + c1*x**3 + c2*cos(c3 + t) + c4*Abs(v)**(1/3) + c5*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`

This has exactly the structure: linear in x, cubic in x, cos(c3+t), Abs(v)**(1/3), and x*Abs(v)**(1/3).

- c0 = A = -6.78570965988404
- c1 = B = -3.39285482994202
- c2 = C = 0.523287159969136
- c3 = -π/2 (so cos(c3 + t) = cos(t - π/2) = sin(t))
- c4 = D = -0.710540944238196
- c5 = E ≈ -0.264876

This matches the GT exactly! ✓
